 pehle match main team ne 307 ran banaae the

 News publishers can now upload instant articles directly to Facebook through their Content Management System (CMS)
 is sarvice ke tahat ab kisi bhi artical ko alag se fasebuk par post nahin karnaa hoga
 For example, if you are posting a story on the website through the content management system, from now on, there will be an option to upload the article to Facebook in the interface of this system
 duusare shabdon main kahen to ab bina wordpress, Joomla or Drupal jaise siemes ko band kiye bina fasebuk par artical daale ja sakenge
 The American newspaper, The Washington Post, has announced that it will upload all the content on Facebook's 'instant Article' service
 gauratlab he ki fasebuk ne duniya kii badi news sansthaanon ke saath qaraar karinstent articalnaam kii sarvice kii shuruyaat kii he
 Through this, articles can be read on Facebook itself
 philhal kisi bhi artical ko puraa padhane ke liye broujar kaa istemaal karnaa hota he
 Facebook has posted ways of posting on its blog
 yahaan siemes se instent artical fasebuk par aplod karne ke liye HTML koding di gai he
 Through this service, Facebook wants to increase more and more content on its site
 fasebuk dwaara jari kiye gaye tareekon main fasebuk ne artical ko behatar or interective tareeke se content aplod karne ke bare main bhi bataaya he

 unka maananaa he ki fasebuk is sarvice se news par bhi apana ekadhikaarwaad banane kaa kaam karegaa
 The state government has become stricter to prevent cheating in Uttar Pradesh Secondary Education Council examinations
 is baar pariksha main nakal karte hue pakade jane par chaatro ko sidhe jail bheja jayega
 Uttar Pradesh Chief Secretary Alok Ranjan has instructed all the district magistrates to take strict steps to conduct the tests without cheating
